CCTV, or closed-circuit television, is used for surveillance and security purposes in various settings, including homes, businesses, and public areas. <span class="posted-on"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2024-10-30T15:07:46+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">October 30, 2024</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/author/admin/" title="View all posts by admin" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">admin</span></a></span></span></div></header><div class="post-image">
<a href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/metal-detectors/">
<img width="740" height="622" src="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Metal-Detectors.jpg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="Metal Detectors" itemprop="image" decoding="async" loading="lazy" srcset="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Metal-Detectors.jpg 740w, https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Metal-Detectors-300x252.jpg 300w, https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Metal-Detectors-600x504.jpg 600w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px" title="Will Stainless Steel Trigger Metal Detectors? </a></div><div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text"><p>Yes, stainless steel can set off metal detectors due to its high iron content. Stainless steel is a common material that can trigger metal detectors and cause false alarms. It is an alloy composed of iron, carbon, and other elements, making it sensitive to metal detection technologies. <a href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/types-of-acl/">
<img width="740" height="493" src="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Types-of-ACL.jpg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="Types of ACL" itemprop="image" decoding="async" loading="lazy" srcset="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Types-of-ACL.jpg 740w, https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Types-of-ACL-300x200.jpg 300w, https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Types-of-ACL-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px" title="How Many Types of ACL are Used for Security? </a></div><div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text"><p>There are three main types of ACLs used for security: standard, extended, and named ACLs. Implementing the appropriate type of ACL is crucial to secure a network from unauthorized access or malicious &#8230; <a title="How Many Types of ACL are Used for Security? <span class="posted-on"><time class="updated" datetime="2025-03-28T12:39:11+00:00" itemprop="dateModified">March 28, 2025</time><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2024-10-18T16:33:03+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">October 18, 2024</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/author/admin/" title="View all posts by admin" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">admin</span></a></span></span></div></header><div class="post-image">

class="entry-title" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/who-invented-biometrics/" rel="bookmark">Who Invented Biometrics? The Best Answer</a></h2><div class="entry-meta">
<span class="posted-on"><time class="updated" datetime="2025-03-28T11:51:42+00:00" itemprop="dateModified">March 28, 2025</time><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2024-09-23T17:43:40+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">September 23, 2024</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/author/admin/" title="View all posts by admin" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">admin</span></a></span></span></div></header><div class="post-image">
<a href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/who-invented-biometrics/">
<img width="513" height="640" src="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/who-invented-biometrics.jpg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="Who Invented Biometrics?" itemprop="image" decoding="async" loading="lazy" srcset="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/who-invented-biometrics.jpg 513w, https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/who-invented-biometrics-240x300.jpg 240w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 513px) 100vw, 513px" title="Who Invented Biometrics? The Best Answer 91">
</a></div><div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text"><p>Biometrics was pioneered in 1858 by Sir William Herschel, a British officer, who began using fingerprints for identification purposes. This revolutionary concept laid the foundation for the development of modern biometric technology. Biometrics refers to the unique biological characteristics of individuals, such as fingerprints, facial features, or iris patterns, used for authentication and identification. Over &#8230; <a title="Who Invented Biometrics? The Best Answer" class="read-more" href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/who-invented-biometrics/" aria-label="Read more about Who Invented Biometrics? class="entry-meta">
<span class="posted-on"><time class="updated" datetime="2025-03-28T11:58:29+00:00" itemprop="dateModified">March 28, 2025</time><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2024-09-19T14:28:24+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">September 19, 2024</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/author/admin/" title="View all posts by admin" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">admin</span></a></span></span></div></header><div class="post-image">
<a href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/basic-structure-of-biometric/">
<img width="1490" height="838" src="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/what-is-the-basic-structure-of-biometric-system.jpg" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" alt="Basic Structure of Biometric" itemprop="image" decoding="async" loading="lazy" srcset="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/what-is-the-basic-structure-of-biometric-system.jpg 1490w, https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/what-is-the-basic-structure-of-biometric-system-300x169.jpg 300w, https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/what-is-the-basic-structure-of-biometric-system-1024x576.jpg 1024w, https://securityequipmentcenter.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/what-is-the-basic-structure-of-biometric-system-768x432.jpg 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1490px) 100vw, 1490px" title="What is the Basic Structure of Biometric System? 92">
</a></div><div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text"><p>The basic structure of a biometric system consists of three main components: the sensor, the feature extraction module, and the matching algorithm. The sensor captures the biometric data, such as fingerprints or facial patterns, which is then processed by the feature extraction module to create a template. The matching algorithm compares this template with stored &#8230; <a title="What is the Basic Structure of Biometric System?" class="read-more" href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/basic-structure-of-biometric/" aria-label="Read more about What is the Basic Structure of Biometric System?">Read more</a></p></div><footer class="entry-meta" aria-label="Entry meta">

<span class="posted-on"><time class="updated" datetime="2025-03-28T12:03:21+00:00" itemprop="dateModified">March 28, 2025</time><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2024-09-12T15:31:29+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">September 12, 2024</time></span> <span class="byline">by <span class="author vcard" itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope><a class="url fn n" href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/author/admin/" title="View all posts by admin" rel="author" itemprop="url"><span class="author-name" itemprop="name">admin</span></a></span></span></div></header><div class="post-image">
<a href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/2-stages-in-a-biometric-system/">

</a></div><div class="entry-summary" itemprop="text"><p>The 2 stages in a biometric system are enrollment and verification. In the enrollment stage, the user&#8217;s biometric data is collected and stored, while in the verification stage, the system compares new biometric data with the stored data to authenticate the user&#8217;s identity. Biometric systems are crucial tools in today&#8217;s security and identification processes. They &#8230; <a title="What are The 2 Stages in a Biometric System?" class="read-more" href="https://securityequipmentcenter.com/2-stages-in-a-biometric-system/" aria-label="Read more about What are The 2 Stages in a Biometric System?">Read more</a></p></div><footer class="entry-meta" aria-label="Entry meta">
